0                                      2              *******************************************************************
                                       3              *                                                                 *

                                       7                       HIBAL
                                     988
                                     989                       SYSDEFN
                                     990              *
                                     991              *
                                     992              *  Modification history:
                                     993              *
                                     994              *    21-April-1997 - M. Durket
                                     995              *
                                     996              *    Fixed a bug in the OPENSETU routine. If the server RPC EXEC
                                     997              *    fails to initialize at startup, then WYLBUR will subsequently
                                     998              *    undergo periodic failsofts in SERVPOST. This is because the
                                     999              *    UNETSVIB field fails to get cleared if the server doesn't
                                    1000              *    initialize. The SVIBUNET field is cleared, though, which
                                    1001              *    triggers the failsoft. One would think that the UNETSVIB
                                    1002              *    field would get closed, because NPATCLS is being called,
                                    1003              *    but there's a call in NPATCLS to check for Suzan posts on
                                    1004              *    the UNET, prior to freeing it - and this calls SERVPOST when
                                    1005              *    it finds that there's a TCP_EOF in the queue.
                                    1006              *
